;;ROP: Notes on temples:
;;temple_of_wisdom uses temple_of_justice levels (like shrine etc) due to incompatibility of carthaginian culture and new temple names
;;Same counts for temple_of_marriage, which has temple_of_law_shrine etc..
;;Same counts for temple_of_sun, which has temple_of_victory_shrine etc..

;;exclusivity tags, used for the "no_building_tagged" condition
tags
{
	temple
}

alias no_other_temple
{
	requires no_building_tagged temple queued

	display_string SMT_TECH_TREE_THREAD_REQUIRES_TEMPLE_DESTRUCTION
}     

building core_building
{
    levels governors_house governors_villa governors_palace proconsuls_palace imperial_palace 
    {
        governors_house requires factions { barbarian, carthaginian, eastern, egyptian, greek, roman, } 
        {
            capability
            {
              law_bonus bonus -5 requires factions { britons, } and hidden_resource judaea
              
              ;;Loyalist revolt CTD fix:
              ;recruit "revolt barbarian peltasts" 0 requires factions { germans, } 
              ;recruit "revolt steppe peltasts" 0 requires factions { scythia, gauls, } 
              ;recruit "revolt eastern spearmen" 0 requires factions { saba, }

              ;recruit "revolt iranian spearmen" 0 requires factions { baktria, }

              ;recruit "revolt babylon spearmen" 0 requires factions { britons, }

              ;recruit "revolt makedon spearmen" 0 requires factions { macedon, } 
              ;recruit "revolt media strukhatian spearmen" 0 requires factions { armenia, } 
            }
            construction  2 
            cost  400 
            settlement_min village
            upgrades

                governors_villa
            }
        }
        governors_villa requires factions { barbarian, carthaginian, eastern, egyptian, greek, roman, }

              agent diplomat  0  requires factions { roman, } 
              law_bonus bonus -5 requires factions { britons, } and hidden_resource judaea

;;ROP Government System
;;There are three government types in action: 
;;Monarchy (power of one)
;;Oligarchy (power of the few)
;;Democracy (power of the many)

;;Democracy is kind of dormant in the beginning of the campaign, but Athens 
;;will create a liking for this govt type later on, thus it *may* spread around.
;;Oligarchy and Monarchy are widespread amongst lots of factions

;;Oligarchy
building hinterland_preq_gov_oligarchy
{
    classification core
    icon government
    levels preq_gov_oligarchy
    {
        preq_gov_oligarchy requires factions { greek, roman, barbarian, egyptian, eastern, carthaginian, } and hidden_resource not_here 
        {
            capability
            {
            }
            construction  1 
            cost  0 
            settlement_min town
            upgrades
            {
            }
        }
    }
    plugins 
    {
    }
}
building gov_oligarchy
{
    classification core
    icon government
    levels gov_oligarchy1 gov_oligarchy2 gov_oligarchy3 gov_oligarchy4 gov_oligarchy5
    {
        gov_oligarchy1 requires factions { all, } and building_present_min_level hinterland_preq_gov_oligarchy preq_gov_oligarchy 
        {
            capability
            {
                religious_belief oligarchy 1
                recruits_exp_bonus bonus 1
            }
            construction  2 
            cost  400

              gov_oligarchy2
            }

              gov_oligarchy3
            }

              gov_oligarchy4

building defenses
{
    levels wooden_pallisade wooden_wall stone_wall large_stone_wall epic_stone_wall 
    {
        ; macedon - makedon
        ; kyrene - kyrene
        ; spain - ionia
        ; dacia - taras
        ;wooden_pallisade requires factions { barbarian, carthaginian, eastern, parthia, egyptian, roman, macedon, kyrene, spain, dacia, seleucid, } or factions { greek_cities, } and not hidden_resource sparta 
        wooden_pallisade requires factions { barbarian, carthaginian, greek, egyptian, eastern, roman, } ;and not hidden_resource sparta
        {
            capability
            {
                law_bonus bonus 1
                wall_level 0
                tower_level 1
            }
            construction  4 
            cost  400 
            settlement_min town
            upgrades
            {
                wooden_wall
            }
        }
        ;wooden_wall requires factions { barbarian, carthaginian, eastern, parthia, egyptian, roman, macedon, kyrene, spain, dacia, seleucid, } or factions { greek_cities, } and not hidden_resource sparta 
        wooden_wall requires factions { barbarian, carthaginian, greek, egyptian, eastern, roman, } ;and not hidden_resource sparta
        {
            capability
            {
                law_bonus bonus 2
                wall_level 1
                gate_strength 1
                tower_level 1
            }
            construction  6 
            cost  800 
            settlement_min large_town
            upgrades
            {
                stone_wall
            }
        }
        ;stone_wall requires factions { carthaginian, eastern, parthia, egyptian, roman, macedon, kyrene, spain, dacia, seleucid, } or factions { greek_cities, } and not hidden_resource sparta 
        stone_wall requires factions { carthaginian, greek, egyptian, eastern, roman, } ;and not hidden_resource sparta
        {
            capability
            {
                law_bonus bonus 3
                wall_level 2
                tower_level 1
                gate_defences 1
                gate_strength 1
            }
            construction  8 
            cost  1600 
            settlement_min city
            upgrades
            {
                large_stone_wall
            }
        }
        ;large_stone_wall requires factions { carthaginian, eastern, parthia, egyptian, roman, macedon, kyrene, spain, dacia, seleucid, } or factions { greek_cities, } and not hidden_resource sparta 
        large_stone_wall requires factions { carthaginian, greek, egyptian, eastern, roman, } ;and not hidden_resource sparta
        {
            capability
            {
                law_bonus bonus 4
                wall_level 3
                tower_level 1
                gate_defences 2
                gate_strength 2
            }
            construction  10 
            cost  3200 
            settlement_min large_city
            upgrades
            {
                epic_stone_wall
            }
        }
        ; only babylon can build this epic stone wall in the city of babylon
        epic_stone_wall requires factions { britons, } and hidden_resource city_babylon
        {
            capability
            {
                law_bonus bonus 5
                wall_level 4
                tower_level 2
                gate_defences 2
                gate_strength 2
            }
            construction  12 
            cost  6400 
            settlement_min huge_city
            upgrades
            {
            }
        }
    }
    plugins 
    {
    }
}

;;Vanilla Barracks. This isn't used in ROP anymore. Instead, we have faction-specific barracks.
building barracks
{
    levels muster_field militia_barracks city_barracks army_barracks royal_barracks 
    {
        muster_field requires factions { slave, } 
        {
            capability
            {
              ;;None anymore :)
            }
            construction  4 
            cost  600 
            settlement_min town
            upgrades
            {
                militia_barracks
            }
        }
        militia_barracks requires factions { slave, } 
        {
            capability
            {
              ;;None anymore :)
            }
            construction  6 
            cost  1200 
            settlement_min large_town
            upgrades
            {
                city_barracks
            }
        }
        city_barracks requires factions { slave, } 
        {
            capability
            {
              ;;None anymore :)          
            }
            construction  8 
            cost  2400 
            settlement_min city
            upgrades
            {
                army_barracks
            }
        }
        army_barracks requires factions { slave, } 
        {
            capability
            {  
              ;;None anymore :)          
            }
            construction  12 
            cost  4800 
            settlement_min large_city
            upgrades
            {
                royal_barracks
            }
        }
        royal_barracks requires factions { slave, } 
        {
            capability
            {
              ;;None anymore :)
            }
            construction  14 
            cost  9600 
            settlement_min huge_city
            upgrades
            {
            }
        }
    }
    plugins 
    {
    }
}

;;ROP FACTION-SPECIFIC BARRACKS GUIDE
;;Two types of recruitment 
;;-homeland Barracks: Local AOR troops available here, filled up with some of your own units in the top tier
;;-Colonial Barracks: All of your own units available. (almost) never local AOR - maybe exceptions in the top tier
;;
;;
;;First level always gives access to lowest tier local AOR - when you colonize, you lose access to them
;;What you can build, depends on your faction\'s style.
;;
;;Colonizing factions like the Greeks:
;;-muster_field upgradeable to colonial or homeland. homeland almost nowhere, Colonial almost everywhere.
;;-homeland hidden_resource example: "and hidden_resource aor_greeks_colonial_available"
;;
;;Assimilating factions like the Persians:
;;-muster_field upgradeable to colonial or homeland. Colonial only in homeland, rest is homeland. 
;;-homeland hidden_resource example: "and not hidden_resource aor_ownfaction"
;;-Highest tier homeland could gives many units you would have when colonizing the region, but should then take alot of time and money to build


;;Greeks
;;For greek factions, the Colonial barracks tree represents the barracks outside the homeland.
;;Both branches have the same effect, but colonizing non-greek land obviously takes somewhat longer to accomplish.
;;If a different Greek faction already colonized a region to a large extent (large_homeland_barracks level), 
;;you don't have to do this again and will get access to the homeland variant.

;;Dorian Greek Barracks
building hinterland_barracks_sparte
{
    classification military
    icon infantry
    levels conquest_barracks homeland_barracks large_homeland_barracks urban_homeland_barracks 
    {
        conquest_barracks requires factions { greek_cities, } and building_present_min_level gov_oligarchy gov_oligarchy1 or factions { greek_cities, } and building_present_min_level gov_monarchy gov_monarchy1 or factions { greek_cities, } and building_present_min_level gov_democracy gov_democracy1 
        {
            capability
            {
                law_bonus bonus 1 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                recruit "campa greek dorian hoplites" 0 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                recruit "campa greek skirmishers" 0 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
            }
            construction  2 
            cost  600 
            settlement_min town
            upgrades
            {
                homeland_barracks
            }
        }
        homeland_barracks requires factions { greek_cities, } 
        {
            capability
            {   
                law_bonus bonus -1 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                trade_base_income_bonus bonus 2 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                recruit "campa greek dorian hoplites" 0 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                recruit "campa greek skirmishers" 0 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                recruit "campa greek archers" 0 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                recruit "campu sparte heavy peltasts" 0 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
            }
            construction  6 
            cost  1200 
            settlement_min large_town
            upgrades
            {
                large_homeland_barracks
            }
        }
        large_homeland_barracks requires factions { greek_cities, } 
        {
            capability
            {
                law_bonus bonus -2 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                trade_base_income_bonus bonus 3 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                recruit "campa greek dorian hoplites" 0 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                recruit "campa greek skirmishers" 0 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                recruit "campa greek archers" 0 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                recruit "campu sparte heavy peltasts" 0 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                recruit "campa greek heavy hoplites" 0 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
            }
            construction  8 
            cost  2400 
            settlement_min city
            upgrades
            {
                urban_homeland_barracks
            }
        }
        urban_homeland_barracks requires factions { greek_cities, } 
        {
            capability
            {
                law_bonus bonus 5 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                trade_base_income_bonus bonus -1 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                recruits_morale_bonus bonus 1 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                population_growth_bonus bonus -3 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                recruit "campa greek dorian hoplites" 0 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                recruit "campa greek skirmishers" 0 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                recruit "campa greek archers" 0 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                recruit "campu sparte heavy peltasts" 0 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                recruit "campa greek heavy hoplites" 0 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                recruit "campa greek cavalry" 0 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                
                ;;Next Level:
                recruit "campu sparte hoplites" 0 requires factions { greek_cities, } 
                recruit "campu sparte heavy hoplites" 0 requires factions { greek_cities, } and hidden_resource sparta 
            }
            construction  12 
            cost  4000 
            settlement_min large_city
            upgrades
            {
            }
        }
    }
    plugins 
    {
    }
}

{
    classification military

    {
        conquest_barracks requires factions { dacia, } and building_present_min_level gov_oligarchy gov_oligarchy1 or factions { dacia, } and building_present_min_level gov_monarchy gov_monarchy1 or factions { dacia, } and building_present_min_level gov_democracy gov_democracy1
        {

                recruit "custa syrako spearmen" 0 requires factions { dacia, }

                recruit "custa rasna axemen" 0 requires factions { dacia, } and hidden_resource aor_oscan

        {

                recruit "campa greek ionian hoplites" 0 requires factions { seleucid, } 
                recruit "campa greek skirmishers" 0 requires factions { seleucid, }

                homeland_barracks
            }
        }

        {
            capability
            {   
                law_bonus bonus 1 requires factions { seleucid, } 
                trade_base_income_bonus bonus 1 requires factions { seleucid, }

                recruit "campa greek skirmishers" 0 requires factions { seleucid, } 
                recruit "campa greek archers" 0 requires factions { seleucid, } 
                recruit "campu greek heavy peltasts" 0 requires factions { seleucid, }

;;Makedon, Northern Greek, pure annexation faction
building hinterland_barracks_makedon
{
    classification military
    icon infantry
    levels conquest_barracks homeland_barracks large_homeland_barracks urban_homeland_barracks 
    {
        conquest_barracks requires factions { macedon, } and building_present_min_level gov_oligarchy gov_oligarchy1 or factions { macedon, } and building_present_min_level gov_monarchy gov_monarchy1 or factions { macedon, } and building_present_min_level gov_democracy gov_democracy1
        {
            capability
            {
;;Available at barracks level 1 and up: Basic AOR
                recruit "campa african archers" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_african
                recruit "campa african spearmen" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_african
                recruit "campa babylon slingers" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_babylon
                recruit "campa babylon spearmen" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_babylon
                recruit "campa barbarian peltasts" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_barbarian
                recruit "campa barbarian slingers" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_barbarian
                recruit "campa eastern slingers" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_eastern
                recruit "campa eastern spearmen" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_eastern
                recruit "campa greek dorian hoplites" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_greek and hidden_resource special_1
                recruit "campa greek ionian hoplites" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_greek and hidden_resource special_2
                recruit "campa greek skirmishers" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_greek
                recruit "campa iranian archers" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_iranian
                recruit "campa iranian spearmen" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_iranian
                recruit "campa kemet lybian archers" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_kemet
                recruit "campa kemet troopers" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_kemet
                recruit "campa lydia karian hoplites" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_lydia and hidden_resource special_3
                recruit "campa lydia mysians" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_lydia and hidden_resource special_2
                recruit "campa lydia pamphylian hoplites" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_lydia and hidden_resource special_5
                recruit "campa lydia phrygians" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_lydia and hidden_resource special_1
                recruit "campa magadh royal guards" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_indian
                recruit "campa magadh skirmishers" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_indian
                recruit "campa makedon skirmishers" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_macedon
                recruit "campa makedon swordsmen" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_macedon
                recruit "campa media strukhatian spearmen" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_media
                recruit "campa media strukhatian archers" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_media
                recruit "campa parsa archers" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_persia
                recruit "campa parsa spearmen" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_persia
                recruit "campa steppe peltasts" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_steppe
                recruit "campa steppe slingers" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_steppe
                recruit "campa thrake peltasts" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_thrake
                recruit "campa thrake slingers" 0 requires factions { macedon, } and hidden_resource aor_thrake
            }
            construction  2 
            cost  600 
            settlement_min town
            upgrades
